   - Super classes: "Thing"

   - This is closer in name and anatomical location to the ventroanterior nucleus of the thalamus. It is likely more relevant than others.

   - Super classes: "brainstem nucleus"
   - Related Synonyms: none listed.
   - While the name includes "anterior," it is a brainstem nucleus, which may not be directly aligned with the thalamus.
